# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-103">통화 품질 대시보드에서 사용할 수 있는 크기 및 측정</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-104">Microsoft 팀 및 비즈니스용 Skype Online에 대 한 CQD (통화 품질 대시보드)는 이러한 서비스를 사용 하 여 발생 하는 통화의 품질을 보다 잘 이해할 수 있도록 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-105">이 항목에서는 CQD를 통해 표시 되는 크기 및 측정값에 대 한 자세한 정보를 제공 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-106">CQD에 대 한 자세한 내용은 [Microsoft 팀 및 비즈니스용 Skype Online에 대 한 통화 품질 대시보드 켜기 및 사용](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)을 참조 하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-107">첫 번째 및 두 번째 끝점 분류</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-108">CQD의 여러 차원과 측정값에는 첫 또는 초로 레이블이 지정 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-109">다음 논리는 스트림이나 통화와 관련 된 끝점에 첫 번째 레이블을 지정 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-110">서버 끝점 (AV MCU, 중재 서버 등)은 서버가 스트림이나 통화에 참여 하는 경우 가장 먼저 고려 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-111">스트림이 두 서버 끝점 사이에 있지 않은 경우 클라이언트 끝점은 초로 간주 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-112">두 종점이 모두 같은 형식이 면 사용자 에이전트 범주의 내부 순서에 따라 첫 번째와 초를 설정 하 여 순서가 일관 되도록 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-113">예를 들어 각 행은 스트림에 관련 된 사용자 에이전트 쌍을 나타냅니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-114">발신자의 사용자 에이전트 범주</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-115">호출 수신자의 사용자 에이전트 범주</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-116">첫 번째 끝점</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-117">두 번째 끝점</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-118">첫 번째 호출자</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-119">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-120">OC (비즈니스용 Skype 클라이언트)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-121">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-122">OC (비즈니스용 Skype 클라이언트)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-123">FALSE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-123">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-124">OC (비즈니스용 Skype 클라이언트)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-124">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-125">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-125">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-126">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-126">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-127">OC (비즈니스용 Skype 클라이언트)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-127">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-128">해제</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-128">FALSE</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-134">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-134">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-135">중재 서버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-135">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-136">중재 서버</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-136">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-137">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-137">AV-MCU</span></span> ||

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-153">첫 번째와 두 번째 분류는 호출자 또는 호출 수신자의 끝점과 구분 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-153">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-154">첫 번째 Is 호출자 차원은 호출자 또는 호출 수신자의 끝점을 식별 하는 데 도움이 될 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-154">The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-155">차원의</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-156">차원 정보는 CQD 포털에 업로드 된 데이터 부분을 기반으로 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-157">여러 차원 값을 필터로 사용할 수도 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-158">다음 표에는 보고서를 만들거나 이전에 정의 된 보고서를 편집 하는 데 사용 되는 쿼리 편집기에 나열 된 순서 대로 CQD에서 현재 사용할 수 있는 차원이 나와 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-159">이름</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-159">Name</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-160">데이터 형식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-160">Data type</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-161">설명</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-161">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-162">빈 값을 사용할 수 있는 이유</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-162">Possible Reasons for blank values</span></span> |
|:---  |:---        |:---         |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-163">**엔드포인트**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-163">**Endpoint**</span></span>|||
| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-164">첫 번째 CPU 이름</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-164">First CPU Name</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-165">문자열</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-165">String</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-166">첫 번째 끝점에 사용 되는 CPU의 이름입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-166">Name of the CPU used by the first endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-167">**예제 값:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-167">**Example value:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span></span> | <br/><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-168">&bull;이 데이터는 끝점에서 보고 되지 않았습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-168">&bull; This data was not reported by the endpoint</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-169">두 번째 CPU 이름</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-169">Second CPU Name</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-170">문자열</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-170">String</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-171">두 번째 끝점에 사용 되는 CPU의 이름입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-171">Name of the CPU used by the second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-172">**예제 값:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-172">**Example value:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span></span> | <br/><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-173">&bull;이 데이터는 끝점에서 보고 되지 않았습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-173">&bull; This data was not reported by the endpoint</span></span>     |

HTTP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2183">DIRECT : HTTP</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2184">실패: 실패</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2186">HTTP: 릴레이</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2186">HTTP : RELAY</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2187">:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2187">:</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2188">: DIRECT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2188">: DIRECT</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2189">: 실패</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2189">: FAILED</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2190">: HTTP</span><span <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2192">각 끝점에 사용 되는 ICE 연결 유형 쌍입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2192">Pair of type of ICE connectivity used by each endpoint.</span></span>   | <span reported</span></span>   |

| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2199">테 넌 트 Id 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2199">Tenant Id Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2200">열거 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2200">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2201">첫 번째와 두 번째 끝점에 대 한 테 넌 트 id 쌍입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2201">Pair of the tenant ids for first and second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2202">**예제 값:** 00000000-0000-0000-0000, 000000000000:00000000, 0000-0000-0000 — 000000000000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2202">**Example value:** 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000 : 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000</span></span>  |  <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2203">&bull;테 넌 트 식별자를 확인할 수 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2203">&bull; The tenant identifier could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2204">이 문제는 종점이 온-프레미스 비즈니스용 Skype 서버 배포에 로그인 한 경우에 발생할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2204">This may happen if endpoint is signed in to an on-premise Skype for Business Server deployment.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2205">건물 이름 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2205">Building Name Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2206">열거 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2206">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2207">첫 번째와 두 번째 끝점에 대 한 건물 이름 쌍입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2207">Pair of the building name for the first and second endpoint.</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2208">&bull;끝점의 건물 이름을 확인할 수 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2208">&bull; The building name for an endpoint could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2209">끝점은 회사 네트워크 외부에 위치 하거나 서브넷 매핑 없이 사이트에서 네트워크에 액세스 하는 것입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2209">This could be because the endpoint is located outside the corporate network, or is accessing the network from a site without a subnet mapping.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2210">**예제 값:** 기본 건물: 지사 사이트 빌드</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2210">**Example value:** Main Building : Branch Site Building</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2211">내부 Corp 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2211">Inside Corp Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2212">열거 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2212">Enumerated pair</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2213">**사용할 수 있는 값:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2213">**Possible values:**</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2214">안쪽: 안쪽</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2214">Inside : Inside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2215">안쪽: 바깥쪽</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2215">Inside : Outside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2216">바깥쪽: 바깥쪽</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2216">Outside : Outside</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2217">끝점이 서브넷 매핑을 기준으로 회사 네트워크 내부 또는 외부에 있는지 여부를 표시 하는 쌍입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2217">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping.</span></span>   |   |
| <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2218">시나리오 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2218">Scenario Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2219">열거 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2219">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2220">끝점이 서브넷 매핑과 네트워크 연결 세부 정보를 기준으로 회사 네트워크 내부 또는 외부에 있는지 여부를 표시 하는 쌍입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2220">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping and the network connection detail.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2221">**참고:** 쌍은 '--'으로 구분 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2221">**Note:** The pairs are separated by '--'.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2222">**예제 값:** 클라이언트 내부-wifi-인사이드</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2222">**Example value:** Client-Inside--Client-Inside-wifi</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2223">&bull;두 끝점 중 하나 또는 둘 다에 대해 네트워크 연결 유형을 알 수 없습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2223">&bull; The network connectivity type was unknown for either or both endpoints.</span></span>  |
||||

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2224">차원 데이터 형식/단위에 대 한 참고 사항</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2224">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2225">부울</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2225">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2226">부울 값은 항상 True 또는 False입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2226">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2227">경우에 따라 True가 1로 표시 되 고 False가 0으로 표시 될 수도 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2227">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2228">범위</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2228">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2229">범위 또는 값 그룹으로 제공 되는 차원은 다음 형식을 사용 하 여 표시 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2229">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2230">_\<정렬 순서 문자열\> [\<하한값 포함\> - \<상한 상한값 전용\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2230">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2231">예를 들어 기간 (분) 차원은 값 범위로 보고 되는 값을 사용 하 여 통화 시간 (초)을 나타냅니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2231">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2232">기간 (분)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2232">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2233">해석 하는 방법</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2233">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2234">062: [0-0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2234">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2235">스트림 기간 = 0 분</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2235">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2236">064: [1-2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2236">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2237">1 분 < = 스트림 기간 < 2 분</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2237">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2238">065: [2-3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2238">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2239">2 분 < = 스트림 기간 < 3 분</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2239">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2240">066: [3-4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2240">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2241">3 분 < = 스트림 기간 < 4 분</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2241">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2242">\<정렬 순서 문자열>는 데이터를 발표할 때 정렬 순서를 제어 하는 데 사용 되며 필터링에 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2242">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2243">예를 들어 기간 (분)에 대 한 필터 < "065" 이면 기간이 2 분 미만인 스트림을 표시 합니다 (필터가 예상 대로 작동 하려면 선행 ' 0 '이 필요 함).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2243">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2244">정렬 순서 문자열의 실제 값이 중요 하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2244">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2245">열거형 문자열</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2245">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2246">CQD에 사용 되는 문자열은 종종 데이터 파일에서 파생 되며, 허용 된 길이 내에서 거의 모든 문자 조합이 될 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2246">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2247">일부 차원은 문자열 처럼 보이지만 미리 정의 된 값의 간단한 목록 중 하나만 사용할 수 있으므로 이러한 열거형은 진정한 문자열이 아닙니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2247">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2248">일부 열거형 문자열도 쌍으로 사용 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2248">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2249">열거 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2249">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2250">열거 쌍으로 제공 되는 차원은 다음 형식을 사용 하 여 표시 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2250">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2251">_\<한 끝점의 열거 값\> : \<다른 끝점의 열거 값\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2251">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2252">열거형 값의 순서는 일관 되지만 첫 번째 또는 두 번째 끝점의 순서는 반영 되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2252">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2253">예를 들어 네트워크 연결 세부 정보 쌍은 두 끝점에 대 한 네트워크 연결 정보 값을 표시 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2253">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2254">네트워크 연결 세부 정보 쌍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2254">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2255">해석 하는 방법</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2255">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2256">유선: 유선</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2256">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2257">첫 번째와 두 번째 끝점은 모두 유선 이더넷 연결을 사용 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2257">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2262">빈 값</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2262">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2263">위의 표에서는 차원이 비어 있을 수 있는 이유를 나열 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2263">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2264">체감 품질 Record 사용 가능 차원이 false 인 경우 많은 치수와 측정이 비어 있게 됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2264">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2265">이는 일반적으로 통화가 성공적으로 설정 되지 않은 경우에 발생 합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2265">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2786">필터가</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2786">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2787">여러 치수 및 측정 값을 필터로 사용할 수도 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2787">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8d3fd-2788">쿼리에 필터를 사용 하 여 차원 또는 측정값을 선택 하는 것과 같은 방식으로 정보를 제거 하 여 쿼리에 정보를 추가 하거나 포함할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8d3fd-2788">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
